< review>
ordered cookies 3 days in advance to pick up 10 boxes  of Christmas cookies at the suggestion of a friend.  Called in my order to speak to a rude girl who gave the impression that she was doing me a favor by selling me $200.00 work of cookies?  Told me they were "booked up till 3 pm" for me to pickup my cookie order.  Upon arrival, there was no one in the bakery except employees.  the same rude girl was at the front counter for me to pay for the cookie order.  the cookies were not ready for my pick up so I ordered a single cookie from the case while I waited. She did not listen to what I asked for and gave me the wrong cookie. After paying, I looked into the bag to find that I had been given the wrong cookie as I reached into the bag.  I had to say excuse me several times before she acknowledged me...I told her that she gave me the wrong cookie I asked for...she offered to take the cookie but I told her I had touched it. so she sold me the correct cookie instead of offering me a free cookie for HER mistake???  After leaving with my order, I contacted the owner Susan Campitelli to suggest that maybe this rude girl should not be the first impression when a customer calls or comes into her store. She  basically offer no concern for the rude girl in the front of her store explaining that they are so busy this time of year??  I will never go back and the friend who referred me, her husband called in an order as well getting the same rude girl in which he was made to feel like he was inconveniencing this rude girl with his order for his business contacts. These are cookies, they need to appreciate the fact that they are busy, (if in fact they are that busy) and treat customers with respect...the customers keep them in business...certainly not their rude employee!!</review>

<Review>When you walk in, you feel like you're transported back into simpler times where cellphones didn't exist and all you needed to make you feel better was a cookie. :)

Their cookie display case is mouthwatering, and there are a lot of choices!

Since it was my first time, I dived straight to the "discounted" area where you can get a bag of "Misfits" for $3 (6 random cookies).

Usually these are day-old or broken cookies. My bag didn't have any broken ones though, and it was mostly chocolate chip with 1 Snickerdoodle, and 1 Macadamia White Choco Chip.

THEY WERE SOO GOOOD.

I LOVE CHEWEY cookies, and these were SO CHEWY and MOIST!

Regularly priced cookies are $1.25 each and they're decently sized.

But if there are Misfit bags available, grab them!

My problem with this shop is the time they took to do the repair, the lack of attention to detail, and lack of accountability. My car went in July 8th, and left September 30th (later to be returned for improper repairs). Gabriel kept telling me the car would be ready on a certain date, I would show up on that day, and he would come up with excuses on why the job was not finished. When I finally did get the "ok" to pick up my car, my car was not repaired properly, as it still had a long scratch along the passenger side and also several scratches on the hood that were supposed to be removed when the car was returned to me. It was missing a mud flap, and some small bracket covers in the rear seat were missing. I was also picking up a sound in the rear of the car. I did end up taking the car home for the weekend as I needed to contact the at-fault driver's insurance and my lawyer.
Now, Gabriel tried telling me that the long scratch along the passengers side was extra, and I needed to contact the other divers insurance, but on good faith he would "repair it either ways." I worked for an automotive bodyshop for a few years, so I know how this stuff works. He was paid, and paid well by the at-fault driver's insurance to repair my car to pre-loss condition. He also tried telling me that the deep scratches on the hood were possibly due to a tree I must park my car under. As for the sound I was picking up, he tried stating the alignment was off and I must of hit a curb pretty bad in that weekend I got to drive my car. The biggest mistake on my part was taking the car home over that weekend and giving him an excuse for that sound. Like I said, I worked in a shop and know that at the very least if this were true a TPMS sensor would have turned on in the dash, and causing a sound that bad would require some extensive damage on the rim. He did state that a spring could have loosened up, but then went back to his original accusations. As for the scratches on the hood, I'm not too sure what to conclude with that, but I know some shops have bad practice of removing things off a car and using the hood as a storage unit to place things on.
At this point, I just couldn't wait to get my car back. Dealing with this shop was a complete nightmare. Gabriel left my car as last priority, and left me to assume he was working with the insurance and not the customer. For the most part my paint was eventually repaired (color sanded/buffed). The mudflap he "had already ordered" was never put back on my car, and the little bracket covers on the rear seat were not put back on.

*In conclusion, I would not recommend any family member or friend to take their cars to this shop, especially if it is an insurance job. They work with the insurance and not with you. Gabriel fed so many lies to me, I think he would make a good politician, I didn't believe any of his lies. I only responded back as a politician even when I knew I was being lied to, just to have the repairs done and receive my car back. I will not be returning to this shop, and they have lost future customers with my family alone. So much for life-time Warranty when the owner takes no accountability!

< review>
DON"T judge the shop by the outside. The place is tranquil, the barbers there are kind and are willing to test new styles with you (that is if you guide them). However, the reason I give this shop 3 stars was because I would've preferred a barber who could've known more professional cuts. Also the barbers tend to give 60% focus on your cut and the rest is spent talking off-track, gazing their eyes elsewhere and not on the haircut. I was a walk-in and I had gotten a random barber (no names). It may have been my fault for not choosing the barber of my style. Give it a shot! It may have not been my cup of tea but maybe it is for you!< /review>

Fun place to stop and check out the sculptures peppered throughout the grounds around Christmas Circle Drive.

Though the attractions were closed to the public we pulled over and watched them from a distance. The pictures below were taken last fall when we were there pre COVID.

Christmas circle in Borrego always reminds me of that scene in the Griswold's European vacation.  Stuck in the endless circle & can't get out. Haha!
With that being said, it is a cool spot to have a packed lunch or enjoy a snack you picked up in town, while taking in the scenery.   We normally stop in that area during the winter months. We like to check out the artworks that are around the area. Most can be seen from the roadway but, there are well traveled trails to get up close. Fun way to engage with nature & explore new parts of the desert. Most standard car's can make it. Just go slow & take ur time.  Borrego springs is a beautiful area, help keep it that way. < Rating>

<Text>Every year at the end of October, "Borrego Days" begins. This event has been reoccurring for over 50 yrs. The 3 day event begins on a Friday and lasts through Sunday evening. There is an annual "Miss Borrego Springs" Pageant prior to Fridays kickoff and then on Saturday there is a 9 am Parade. Thru the weekend, there are vendors selling various items such as handmade jewelry, drinks, food, speciality items, toys, a jumper for kids ALL & more at Christmas Circle! I went on Sunday this year and there was a very popular & famous live band from Sinaloa, Mexico. Great Music! Lots of people dancing! Enjoying themselves and sharing with one another! After all, we are a small town of approx. 3500 people. There are many restaurants you can eat at when you come to Borrego. Like Carlees, which has a bar, pool tables, Dinning area, Music & Karioke. There's Pablitos Mexican, Jilbertos Taco Shop, Kendall's Cafe (Which is my favorite place in Borrego, eat in or order by phone for pick up, carry out) El Borrego Mex, Red Ocotillo ( the Hamburgers are SUPERB), Palm Canyon Resort, which just recently changed there menu (and I think it was great and easier to order) and prices very reasonable. They have a Saloon where you can order n eat there as well.. (employees seem intuitive and always smiling) So, put it in your calendar for next year and come on down and enjoy, relax, unwind and share a memorable weekend as a family!!!< /Text><Pics>None< /Pics><resp>None<//resp><GmapID>0x80da34f67e72323f:0x5f503dd725dbbbda<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>

<rating>2<//rating>< text>
I have stayed here twice before, on the other side of the hotel and it was quiet and pleasant, nice amenities at a good price. This stay was quite a different experience. Our room this time was by the pool. When I arrived there were lots of people, outside their rooms, smoking and drinking beers. There was trash and cigarette butts littering the pathways and the grass around the pool area. It was quite an atmosphere. My Ford Escape was one of the nicest cars in the lot and the thought crossed my mind if it would be broken into in the night. The room had some issues this time. The towels were visibly dirty. The shower rail was broken so the curtain wouldn't fully close and the towel hooks were hanging off the wall. The paint was chipped on the walls and it just looked generally worn and run down. One lamp didn't work and the other was cracked and broken on the shade. We decided to use the hot tub around 9pm. There were still lots of people outside, not a problem, but there were little children with seemingly no parental supervision, running around and on skateboards and scooters, screaming and yelling. These kids looked to be around 5 years old and seemed to have no bedtime. Some drunk people got into a fight and I wondered if someone was going to get thrown off the balcony. It was quite entertaining. It was not very relaxing. The hot tub was full of trash, including an unidentified pinkish red object. I am fearful I May have contracted something being in there and took a very hot shower after mistakenly getting it there, lol. This side of the hotel is closer to the busy road. It was very noisy all night long and I was kept awake by this. We were staying here as my boyfriend had had surgery and we needed somewhere to stay overnight. I went to get us food at breakfast to take back to the room for him. I was told that breakfast is dine in only. I had to explain why I needed to take him breakfast before I was allowed to take a small plate of eggs and some yogurt. On the plus side, when I asked for napkins and spoons at the front desk, the girl was very nice, polite and accommodating. If you are looking for a run down, budget, motel type of place, you can find it here. If you are looking for any sort of quality, look elsewhere.< /text>

This place is a real gem for the value-minded. Some of the other locations of this chain that I've been to are much nicer, overall. However, you can tell the rooms have been 'used', and much of the furniture has not replaced in a long time (quite possibly, too long?) But, everything works and is always clean. Overall, if i needed to I would stay here again. It was quiet, clean, no odors, or issues with parking, finding the location or overall customer service. <response>None<//response><text>I was not greeted as a Choice member, though the receptionist was courteous and helpful. The room was adequate, though the carpet was well worn and the walls need new paint.

The hotel offers about twenty cable T.V. channels--MUCH less than most other Choice Hotels I've visited. I called the front desk and was told that the receptionist would inform the manager, but the manager never contacted me and actually said on Trip Advisor that the hotel would "add" the channel (though the room's channel guide listed FOX, supposedly on channel 30).

I have stayed at this property in the past and I will never stay there again!<//text></record>

<Rate>None<//Rate>< Review>
I was on business and stayed several nights. I requested the top floor and stayed on the 3rd floor over the pool. I parked in the back, which had quick access to the elevator. There was always parking available. I found the property on the internet and requested it through my travel agency. It‚Äôs located next to a walking trail on the river. The river was dry while I was there. 

There is a restaurant next door and a gas station down the street. There is a grocery store about 2 miles away. I had a microwave and refrigerator in my room. The hotel is located a block from the interstate. 

The staff were very nice and respectful. The front desk clerk remembered me from a previous stay. The breakfast was good. They had sausage and eggs, cereal, toast, and coffee every morning. They had other food also. 

The room was clean and neat every day. The shower was fine. The TV was good with good volume. I would stay there again.</Review>

We stayed for two nights 08/22 & 08/23/08, we were meeting friends for Bingo at San Manuel. In the past on similar trips had stayed at the Hilton, this time we were looking to save $ on the room. One thing that had made us nervous was a review about the area. There was no problem whatsoever with the area  being a few blocks from the Hilton. The door often required multiple attempts to open, and on the third night, they had deactivated the door key, as the person who checked me in thought I was only staying 2 nights. The wifi was molasses slow, and most sites wouldn't even load. Kept my phone on 4G the entire time I was there. I won't even go into the "small" things, like the cracked air mover cover that rattled when the heat kicked in, or the cigarette burn holes in the curtains (non-smoking room of course).

On the plus side, the bed was quite comfy and the housekeeping did a good job on the one day they appeared.</Text>

< review>
My friend and I arrived at 1 am, tired and weary after work. The front desk was still open and a friendly but efficient clerk checked us in. We must have looked exhausted because the clerk voluntarily tried to find us a room on the ground floor but the best she could find was 2nd floor. There are 3 floors and no elevator. The room was clean, quiet and spacious. We had chosen this hotel because unlike quite a few others in the area, they didn't have any reported issues with bed bugs. Toiletries, a refrigerator, a clock and coffee supplies were provided. All lamps, etc. we're in good working condition. One of the beds was lumpy and past its prime but it didn't affect my sleep. A person with a bad back would have had problems though. An open band wi-fi at average speed was welcome. Plenty of hot water for our showers. We enjoyed the breakfast with many selections, including make your own waffles, in the AM.
I give this hotel 5+ stars based on the fact that I am judging it compared to others in its class. Don't expect a Jaguar when you've bought a Ford Fiesta.< /review>

I chose this place to stay for one night.  Online, the inside pictures somewhat misrepresents the room. I checked in last night. I called ahead for a late check-in. The lady at the front desk was rude! She didn't greet me as I walked in. I am a short woman.  Even after, complaining that the countertop was very high and that I didn't see her when I walked up, she stayed sitting, instead of standing up. She spoke very fast and her mannerisms were not up to par. I had to ask if there were elevators to get me to my room because the lobby is small and I didn't see an elevator. There was no map provided and her explanation of location was hard to understand.

Before I left the lobby, I asked for an extra blanket. She said that they were "out of clean blankets" and that she would find me one later, "around 10pm" but I would have to come back and get it myself. The elevators are located outside. Inside of the elevators stink badly and there is graffiti on the inside wall. Once off of the elevator, I searched for my room and  was not too pleased with the outside upkeep of this property.

When I got inside of my room, I was pleasantly surprised because, just walking in, the room looked nice compared to the outside. After taking a closer look, I noticed that my bedspread, had small cigarette like burns and a little stain on it. The outside bathroom door appears dirty and/or stained staind and in need of replacement. I attempted to watch TV and couldn't find the remote in my room. I called the front desk and asked where it would be placed. Of course with my luck, there was NO REMOTE in my room. The lady at the front desk told me she would have to get one from another room and that I WOULD HAVE TO GO GET IT FROM THE LOBBY. HER reason for asking me to go back and get the remote and blanket was because she was alone. (I have stayed at other establishments, where the hotel rep told me that they were alone and that once they got a free moment, they would bring up my request. So this was new to me)

I attempted to call their quality assurance department, to make a formal complaint, but they were closed. So I called back up to the lobby about 20 mins later to ask if a manager would be on duty. The lady puts me on hold to ask ANOTHER PERSON!!! I was told that there is no manager avail until MONDAY. I proceeded to ask for a general manager's contact information. So again, she asked someone else. Then, the person she was talking to gets on the phone and asks me what's the problem. I explained to her that I am NOT pleased with the level of service in which I have received from the moment of checking in up until that point. I explained that I am a single woman staying at their establishment, it was late and very dark outside and that I had no intentions of going back down to pick up a blanket and a remote to the TV. I was afraid for my safety as the outside did not look like a safe environment and that I didn't even have a car to just leave and find another hotel to stay at. My room was not stay ready, since it did not have everything it needed for my stay and that as a paying customer, it is a big inconvenience to me to ask me to go down at night alone to pick up something that should have been in the room before I arrived and before she took my deposit and swiped my debit card. At this point, the extra blanket was not an issue. She didn't offer an apology. She tokd me to speak with someone named Annette who would be in at 6AM SUNDAY (the morning I'm checking out) but less than 2 mins prior, I was told there was no manager available until MONDAY. I said okay, and before I could even say "thank you" she had already hung up!

I also don't understand why there were now two people working the lobby when I was originally told that the first lady was alone and now since there are two people, why couldn't one of them at least bring up the remote so that I can watch TV in my room because there was only a power but and no other visible buttons on the TV to manually change the channel. The hot water only runs warm.  Terrible experience! #poorservice< /Review>
